-Wear comfortable casuals suitable for a theme park (T-shirts, track pants, shorts, etc.).
-Only synthetic clothes (nylon/polyester) are allowed on water rides.
-Denim, cotton, sarees, dupattas, or salwars are not permitted for water activities.
-Avoid transparent, revealing, or offensive clothing.
-Carry a change of clothes, towel, and waterproof footwear/flip-flops.

💧 Water Park Rules:

-Only synthetic swimwear allowed in water areas.
-Inappropriate attire will prevent access to rides.
-Lockers and changing rooms are available inside.
-Follow all safety instructions and staff directions.
-No outside food or beverages are allowed inside the park.

‎[06/09/2025, 11:05:12 pm] Raj Christ: 💃 Call for Auditions – Team Gujarat 🕺

From the vibrant land of colors and devotion, Team Gujarat is ready to set the stage alive with the energy of Garba and Dandiya Raas! ✨

Rooted in devotion to Goddess Amba, Garba is not just a dance, but a celebration of life, rhythm, and community. With circular formations, graceful hand movements, and swirling traditional attire, the dance embodies joy and spiritual togetherness. 💫

The beats of the dhol and the jingling of dandiyas create a symphony that unites everyone into one vibrant circle of festivity. 💃🪘
Join us as we showcase the essence of Gujarat — where rhythm meets devotion, and every step becomes a prayer in motion. 🙏

We are conducting an experimental study on the Christ BYC campus as part of a PhD research and are inviting student participants.
*When?* November 2025

*What can you expect?*
- Spend around 1 hour, for 2 weeks in November, working on your regular college-related tasks in a supportive environment
- Share your thoughts and experiences through a few short forms
- Contribute to a better understanding of study environments and help us create more effective learning spaces

*Why participate?*
- Gain insights into your own learning habits and productivity
- Be part of a research study that can shape the future of the learning environment 
- Enjoy a relaxed and supportive environment while working on your tasks

Please fill out the short screening form here: *https://forms.gle/eN3GmJUU2uNGodfa9*

Your participation will be greatly valued.

[07/11/2025, 6:52:07 pm] ~ Preeti Kumari: Dear Lakshmi,

As discussed, we are looking for volunteers to support us on-ground for our upcoming EntrepreNaari Mela 2.0.

Event Dates: 3rd & 4th December, 2025
Timings: 8:00 AM – 9:00 PM
Venue: KPTO Industrial Ground, Bengaluru I’m sharing the event details below for your reference:

Aspire For Her in collaboration with GHCI Asia’s largest gathering of women and allies in technology, fueling innovation, career growth, and industry transformation presents EntrepreNaari Mela 2.0.

We are looking for student volunteers to support us on-ground during the Mela days. Our team will personally interact with all selected students to ensure their roles and responsibilities are clearly explained. Additionally, we may require their support in the days leading up to the event—for tasks such as venue checks, stage setup, and other pre-event preparations if any.

Roles and Responsibilities - Please find attached the details.

What it is for the students -
Opportunity to gain hands-on experience in event planning and management.
Exposure to real-world coordination with entrepreneurs, vendors, and partner teams.
Chance to be part of a large-scale social impact event empowering women entrepreneurs.
Opportunity to build teamwork, communication, and leadership skills.
Receive a certificate of participation/internship letter recognizing their contribution.
Network with professionals, mentors, and social impact leaders.
We are also looking for a group of 3–4 creative students to perform on stage — this could be a dance, music, or any cultural performance. It’s a wonderful opportunity for students to showcase their talent in front of a large audience.

The stage dimensions will be shared shortly. Please note that the venue does not have a green room for costume changes, so it would be ideal to plan performances that require no costume changes.

Look forward to an active involvement from the students of Christ College. Thanks so much for your support.

1. State a problem faced by the target audience
2. Intensify the problem
3. Mention your solution + your personal branding statement
4. Mention the value addition you provide
As a first-year Masters student of AI, here’s my response to the above-mentioned points

a) Problem: [Mention the problem]
b) Intensify: [Mention an add-on problem]
c) Solution + personal brand: [Mention your solution + personal brand]
d) Value addition: [Mention 1 value addition you can provide]

I want you to craft an elevator pitch for me using the overcomer technique. It should be simple to understand, crisp and not longer than 90 seconds when being delivered
